! ðŸ‡¸ðŸ‡ª Beskrivning: Den hÃ¤r listan fjÃ¤rnar reklamar och sporing pÃ¥ svensksprÃ¥kiga websidor. Den Ã¤r mycket nÃ¤rt knuten till Â«Frellwit's Swedish FiltersÂ», men har blivit modifiserad fÃ¶r att fjÃ¤rna uppfÃ¶ringer som stridar emot reglementet fÃ¶r inkludering i Adblock Plus (sÃ¥ som anti-anti-adblocking, cookie-notifikationer, nyhetsbrev, med mer), och Ã¶ka kompatibiliteten med ABP 3.x sin syntax, eftersom Frellwits lista inte tilbjuder offisiell brukerstÃ¶d fÃ¶r ABP-brukare. Planen Ã¤r att synkronisera med listan honoms omkring en gÃ¥ng i mÃ¥naden, och att vi i ABP-teamet lÃ¤gger till bÃ¥da variga och mildertidiga fixer i mÃ¤llantiden.
! ðŸ‡¬ðŸ‡§ Description: This list removes advertising and tracking on Swedish-language websites. It is very closely connected to "Frellwit's Swedish Filters", but has been modified to remove entries that are against the rules for inclusion in Adblock Plus (such as anti-anti-adblocking, cookie notifications, newsletters, etc.), and increase compatibility with ABP 3.x's syntax, since Frellwit's list does not offer official user support for ABP users. The plan is to synchronise with his list roughly once a month, and that the ABP team add both permanent and temporary fixes in the meantime.

! ðŸ‡¸ðŸ‡ª Notis: Brukare av alla andra adblockare, spesielt uBlock Origin och AdGuard, vil ha det mycket bÃ¤ttre om dem bruker Frellwits lista direkt i stÃ¤llet, i huvudsak eftersom den brukar uBO-spesifikka egenskapor och mottar vÃ¤ldigt hyppiga uppdateringar.
! ðŸ‡¬ðŸ‡§ Note: Users of any other adblockers, especially uBlock Origin and AdGuard, are much better off using Frellwit's list directly instead, mostly due to it using uBO-specific features and receiving very frequent updates.
